Follow up calls to ensure that they are satisfactorily resolved and maintain call lists at required, minimum, levels. <br>8. Be the primary technical contact for several high profile clients. <br>9. You will be confident in challenging business requirements to ensure you are continuously delivering the best possible outcome, harnessing innovation and driving adoption of new technologies to deliver business value</p> <p><strong>Essential skills and experience:</strong></p> <ul> <li>Programming languages: Python Scripting, knowledge of Java</li> <li>Build tools: knowledge of Gradle (or) Maven</li> <li>Architectural styles: Web services, SOA, REST API, Micro services</li> <li>Code versioning tools: GIT (or) Mercurial</li> <li>Testing: Junit, Mockito, Powermock</li> <li>Java IDE: IntelliJ (or) Eclipse</li> <li>Web framework: Experience in any of the popular webservice frameworks like Spring-ws, CXF, RestEasy</li> <li>Application Lifecycle Management Tools: JIRA, Confluence, Jenkins, NexusPro (or) similar.</li> <li>Working practices: Knowledge and experience of agile frameworks and practices: Scrum/Kanban, user stories, BDD/TDD, DevOps, Continuous Integration &amp; Delivery, Pair Programming etc.</li> <li>BigData Technologies: AWS Aurora, Kerberos, Real Time data processing, Spark, Kafka, Samza</li> <li>Devops: AWS, Kubernetes, Ansible, Jenkins, Groovy, Shell Scripting</li> <li>Kafka, ELK, Aurora DB, Graph</li> </ul> <p><strong>About Cognizant:</strong> Cognizant (Nasdaq-100: CTSH) is one of the world's leading professional services companies, transforming clients'? business, operating and technology models for the digital era. Our unique industry-based, consultative approach helps clients envision, build and run more innovative and efficient businesses. Headquartered in the U.S., Cognizant is ranked 195 on the Fortune 500 and is consistently listed among the most admired companies in the world. </div><div class="visareqtext"></div><div class="clear"></div><div id="md_skills" class="md_skills"><p><strong>Senior QA Engineer, Test Automation, Selenium, Protractor, JavaScript, Cypress</strong></p> <p>We are working with a <strong>highly successful</strong> <strong>Software Company in Maidenhead</strong> who are <strong>seeking a Senior QA Engineer</strong> to help them in their current <strong>mission to Automate all the things </strong> and evolve their technical environment to <strong>achieve 100% automation. </strong>Our client creates <strong>powerful yet elegant software solutions </strong>that utilise <strong>.NET on the Back End</strong> as well as <strong>cutting-edge data visualisation tools</strong> so the ideal Senior QA Engineer will have end-to-end testing experience. The Senior QA Engineer is a role that involves leadership and mentoring but is also very technical and will allow you to <strong>utilise your hands-on skills and lead from the front'.</strong></p> <p>Not only will the new Senior QA Engineer enjoy a stimulating working environment, working on complex software but he/she will also enjoys a<strong> great</strong> <strong>work-life balance with flexible hours and some optional remote work available</strong>. If you're an experienced Software Tester looking for a new challenge with an up-and-coming software company then this Senior QA Engineer vacancy could be a great move for you in your career, with opportunities to grow as the company expands and enjoys continued success!</p> <p><strong>The Main Responsibilities of the Senior QA Engineer include:</strong></p> <ul> <li>Creating <strong>automation test frameworks from scratch</strong>.</li> <li>Contributing to new test strategies, striving to achieve 100% automation through <strong>Continuous Testing</strong> practices.</li> <li>A large amount of time will be spent time writing and executing tests.</li> </ul> <p><strong>What do you need to be suitable?</strong></p> <ul> <li>Have established yourself as a good software tester with a good eye for detail.</li> <li>Experience in Agile teams.</li> <li>Have an in-depth understanding of different SDLCs and are familiar with practices such as TDD, BDD.</li> <li>You will understand the value of and are comfortable with all types of <strong>functional and non-functional testing such as performance and security testing.</strong></li> <li>You will have an excellent understanding of test automation frameworks and have experience working in one or more programming language.</li> <li>You understand software architecture and can exploit it to inform a test approach.</li> </ul> <p><strong>Technology Stack:</strong></p> <ul> <li><strong>Selenium </strong>Web driver</li> <li><strong>Protractor, Cypress, JavaScript</strong></li> <li>Mocha.js, <strong>Nightwatch.js</strong></li> <li>C# or Java Scripting</li> <li>Docker, Octopus, Jenkins</li> <li>Jira, Bitbucket, Git, TestRail</li> <li><strong>Agile</strong>, Waterfall.</li> </ul> <p><strong>Company Benefits</strong></p> <p>New staff will be enrolled and included in the company benefits packages. This is a great package which includes: Private Healthcare, a generous Pension Scheme, Flexible Hours, Remote Working available, 25 days' holiday and the chance to buy additional holiday if required.</p> <p><strong>Location</strong></p> <p>Based in Maidenhead, our client's office is commutable from Slough, High Wycombe, Reading, Woking, Aylesbury, and many more with links to London and Oxford. </p> <p>If you're interested in this position, please APPLY NOW!</p> <p><strong>Senior QA Engineer, Test Automation, Selenium, Protractor, JavaScript, Cypress</strong></p> <p>Referral Scheme: If this role isn't for you then perhaps you could recommend a friend or colleague to Haybrook IT. </div><div class="visareqtext"></div><div class="clear"></div><div id="md_skills" class="md_skills"><p>Job Purpose<br></p><p>The Programme Manager is responsible for the successful coordination and administration of all aspects of new and ongoing programmes including planning, organising, staffing, leading, and controlling programme activities as well as leading engagement with the client to secure value-added opportunities, maximise relationships and build trust.<br>The Programme Manager must have an in-depth knowledge of Programme Management principles and be cognoscente to deliver outcomes against the client's strategic imperatives and maximise the value.</p> <p>Essential characteristics<br></p><p>Delivery:<br> </p><p>Thorough understanding of Programme Management techniques and methodologies<br> Experience of project management practices both Waterfall and Agile <br> Have an in-depth understanding of Retail Supply Chain domain<br> Strong experience of leading and owning delivery work and ongoing improvement plans embracing DevOps and Rapid Release initiatives by delivering quality to our customers faster <br> Ensure that software is built in a way which is consistent with and exploits where possible - the collective frameworks, patterns and best practices that exist across the wider Engineering community within Supply chain domain alongside working with business owners and stakeholders<br> Determine to order of work by assessing the cost/benefit of each product backlog item<br> Responsible for ensuring all decisions are made within a sound risk framework and within Group standards and appetite<br> Responsible for driving automation strategy (testing &amp; deployment)<br> Manage Service level improvement plans<br> Manage Technical debt accounted for every software delivery<br> Agile practitioner<br> Experience of working with a UK Retailer within the Supply Chain domain<br> Should have led delivery teams of minimum 25 people across multiple geographies<br> Minimum 10 years of software project management experience<br> Experience of working in fast-paced &amp; complex customer environments<br> Experience in managing software development projects for Legacy environments as well as cloud</p> <p>Commercial Acumen:<br> </p><p>Business acumen to understand costs and value-driven activities<br> Ability to construct and analyse reports both delivery and financially focussed<br> Create forecasts and budgets to deliver against<br> Managing effectively; budget, time and quality in order to achieve the best ROI</p> <p>Leadership<br> </p><p>Lead a team from offshore and onsite with a mix of technical competencies including Architects, Developers, Testers, Project/Delivery/Test Managers, Business Analysts etc to ensure cohesive teams<br> Mentor individuals across technology disciplines</p> <p>Management<br> </p><p>Individual and team management to ensure the team adheres to Mastek and code of conducts</p> <p>Engagement<br> </p><p>Demonstrate Strong stakeholder and relationship management skills<br> Thorough understanding of engagement techniques demonstrating persuading and influencing skills<br> Excellent communication skills<br> Excellent problem-solving skills</p> <p>Primary Duties and Responsibilities<br></p><p>The Programme Manager performs a wide range of duties and all the following attributes:<br>Plan the programmes<br> Plan the delivery of the overall portfolio and programmes and activities in accordance with the mission and the goals of Mastek<br> Develop new initiatives to support the strategic direction<br> Develop and implement long-term goals and objectives to achieve the successful outcome of the programmes<br> Develop funding proposals for the programme to ensure the continuous delivery of services</p> <p>Organise the programmes<br> </p><p>Ensure that programme activities operate within the policies and procedures<br> Ensure that programme activities comply with all relevant legislation and professional standards</p> <p>Resource the programmes<br> </p><p>Recruit, interview and select well-qualified individuals across all skillsets<br> Implement the human resources policies, procedures and practices<br> Assist individuals to achieve their personal goals and development plans</p> <p>Lead the programmes<br> </p><p>Lead the team by providing strategic direction, input and feedback<br> Communicate with clients and other stakeholders to gain community support for the programme and to solicit input to improve the programmes<br> Liaise with other managers to ensure effective and efficient programme delivery<br> Coordinate the delivery of services among different programme activities to increase effectiveness and efficiency<br> Ensure quality management systems are in place for constraints, assumptions, risks, dependencies and issues</p> <p>Governance and Control the programmes<br> </p><p>As part of the Account Leadership Team, instigate the growth targets and account development opportunities <br> Create reports on the programme for Mastek and the customer<br> Communicate with sponsors as outlined in contractual/work package agreements<br> Ensure that the programmes operate within the approved budget<br> Monitor and approve all budgeted programme expenditures<br> Monitor margin projections and margin variance <br> Manage all project funds according to established accounting policies and procedures<br> Ensure reports and supporting documentation for sponsors are prepared<br> Provide required information to create and submit invoices to clients<br> Identify and evaluate the issues and risks associated with programme activities and take appropriate actions<br> Monitor the programme activities on a regular basis and conduct regular evaluations<br> Report evaluation findings and recommend changes to enhance the programmes</p> <p>Personal characteristics<br></p><p>The Programme Manager should demonstrate competence in all the following attributes:<br> </p><p>Behave Ethically: </p><p>Understand ethical behaviour and business practices, and ensure that own behaviour and the behaviour of others is consistent with these standards and aligns with the values of the organisation<br> </p><p>Engages and Build Relationships: </p><p>Establish and maintain positive working relationships with others, both internally and externally, to achieve the goals of the organisation<br> </p><p>Communicate Effectively: </p><p>Communicate in a timely manner using appropriate and effective tools and techniques<br> </p><p>Creativity/Innovation: </p><p>Develop new and unique ways to improve operations of the organisation and to create new opportunities<br> </p><p>Focus on Client Needs: </p><p>Anticipate, understand, and respond to the needs of internal and external clients to meet or exceed their expectations within the organisational parameters<br> </p><p>Foster Teamwork: </p><p>Work collaboratively to set goals, resolve problems, and make decisions that enhance the account and organisational effectiveness<br> </p><p>Servant Leadership: </p><p>Enable, empower and support the team; positively influence them to achieve results that are in the best interest of the client and organisation<br> </p><p>Make Decisions: </p><p>Assess situations to determine the importance, urgency and risks, and make clear decisions which are timely and in the best interests of the client and organisation<br> </p><p>Organize: </p><p>Set priorities, develop a work schedule, monitor progress towards goals, and track details, data, information and activities<br> </p><p>Plan: </p><p>Determine strategies to add value to the client and organisation, set goals, create and implement actions plans, and evaluate the process and results<br> </p><p>Solve Problems: </p><p>Assess problem situations to identify causes, gather and process relevant information, generate possible solutions, and make recommendations and/or resolve the problem</p> <p>Essential skills, qualifications and experience required to be able to perform the role<br> </p><p> Skills<br> </p><p>Managing Successful Programs<br> Knowledge of well documented patterns and techniques for filling in the intentional gaps left in the Scrum approach (example: numerous Burndown techniques, numerous Retrospective formats, handling bugs, etc)<br> Experience playing the Scrum Master/Product Owner role for number of years for software development teams that was diligently applying Scrum principles, practices, and theory.<br> Supply Chain, Manufacturing, Finance and Logistics domain knowledge is essential.<br> Must have proven experience of project deliveries in different capacities in a financial or supply chain industry in both </div><div class="visareqtext"></div><div class="clear"></div><div id="md_skills" class="md_skills"><p>Fixed Term Contract - 102 weeks</p><p>As a DevOps Engineer, you will have experience of designing and architecting highly available services on a cloud platform such as AWS or Azure, and implementing continuous integration technologies such as Jenkins, and orchestration tools such as Ansible or Terraform.</p><p>As a DevOps Engineer, you will work to optimise our development processes and identify process optimisation opportunities and contribute to the implementation of proposed solutions. You will initially work mostly with AWS or Azure developing and supporting systems and infrastructure through to production using modern continuous integration/deployment (CI/CD) techniques and supporting analysis, identification, prioritisation and implementation of incremental improvements to our services currently running. You will be a good technical communicator, able to improve developer experience through tools and technologies in collaboration with the development teams throughout the development lifecycle to live service and decommissioning. You will maintain the security, confidentiality and integrity of our cloud services by implementing relevant information security standards and ensure compliance with relevant legislations and regulations.</p><p><strong>Main Duties and Responsibilities </strong></p><ol><li>Lead development and rollout of a continuous integration and deployment pipeline across the Digital's estate of apps and services, use of containerisation techniques where appropriate, and working collaboratively with other departments</li><li>Support developers, system administrators and technical architects to use DevOps approaches to design, architect, automate and implement highly available and fault-tolerant environments (staging, quality assurance, user acceptance and production), with multi-cloud capability primarily starting on AWS or Azure</li><li>Work with technical colleagues to define and implement DevOps methodology using practices recommended in the GDS Digital by Default Service Standard. Support the team to extend our continuous integration pipeline across our estate of mobile and web apps</li><li>Write infrastructure as code for AWS or Azure. Use cross-platform APIs and automation/deployment technologies such as Ansible or similar to orchestrate cloud platform deployments</li><li>Support and fix bugs in existing application deployment pipelines, using standard debugging tools to track down and identify root causes. Work independently to find solutions/identify problems and to work with the Lead and Senior Developers to solve more challenging issues</li><li>Review existing applications, advising and supporting colleagues on configuring and converting them for deployment to the cloud or migrate from other cloud providers. Support setting up continuous integration/deployment, developing automation scripts and advising developers on adapting them to run in the cloud</li><li>Working in sprints in a multidisciplinary scrum team, collaborate and liaise with delivery managers, product owners and other stakeholders to identify business requirements and implement user stories</li><li>Collaborate and work with external developers and cloud service providers to ensure PHE derives the maximum benefit from any third-party service providers and that the right knowledge is transferred in-house</li><li>Continuously seek to improve your own knowledge of work areas, bringing your learning back into the team, and embrace the agile framework of software delivery. Support colleagues to reach full agility using DevOps best practices including continuous integrations, delivery, and release</li><li>Consistently work to meet project deadlines and manage time effectively to deliver projects on budget</li></ol><p>Essential Skills</p><ul><li>Educated to degree level in relevant subject such as computer science with core development element or equivalent level qualification or experience of working at a similar level in specialist area</li><li>Proficiency/experience with DevOps approaches to application testing and deployment</li><li>Experience of automated deployment of applications and services to AWS or Azure</li><li>Design, development and support of CI/CD pipelines (eg Jenkins) in a microservice architecture</li><li>Knowledge/experience of appropriate standards, methods and tools to design systems using DevOps principles</li><li>Knowledge/experience of cloud automation technologies such as Ansible, Terraform or others</li><li>Genuine passion and interest in DevOps and cloud automation technologies and version control software (Git, Bitbucket pipelines, Teamcity)</li><li>Ability to handle multiple tasks, workloads and be an excellent communicator</li><li>Able to identify opportunities to optimise application development/deployment and lifecycle processes and contribute to their implementation using DevOps and Agile approaches</li><li>Able to defines the continuous integration build, co-ordinate build activities across systems and understand how to undertake and support integration testing activities</li><li>Able to work with business and technology stakeholders to translate business problems into technical designs, specifying and designing systems using appropriate standards and tools</li><li>An understanding of and commitment to equality of opportunity and good working relationships, both in terms of day-to-day working practices, but also in relation to management systems</li></ul><p>Desirable skills</p><ul><li>Postgraduate or professional qualification or equivalent experience in of working at a similar level in specialist area</li><li>Experience of containerisation or microservices technologies and techniques, such as Docker or Kubernetes</li><li>Experience of providing software testing services that includes test automation</li><li>Experience of Agile principles, practices and tools such as Jira</li></ul><p></p></div><!-- skills --><div class="clear"></div><div id="jd_mediaUrl" class="jd_mediaUrl"></div><div class="clear"></div><hr><!-- these are the individual job detail The Team depends on the Scrum Master to maintain focus on their commitments, shield them from outside distractions and help them to self-organise and collaborate.</p> <p>The Scrum Master serves the Product Owner in several ways:</p> <ul> <li>Finding techniques for effective Product Backlog Management</li> <li>Clearly communicating Vision, goals and Product backlog items to the Team</li> <li>Teaching the scrum team to create clear and concise Product Backlog items </li> <li>Understanding long-term product planning in an empirical environment</li> <li>Understanding and practicisng agility and</li> <li>Facilitating Scrum events as requested or needed</li> </ul> <p>The Scrum Master serves the agile delivery team in several ways including:</p> <ul> <li>Coaching the team in self-organisation and cross-functionality</li> <li>Teaching and Leading the Team to create high-value products</li> <li>Removing impediments to the Team's progress</li> <li> Facilitating Scrum events as requested or needed and</li> <li>Coaching the Team in organisational environments in which Scrum is not yet fully adopted and understood</li> </ul> <p>The Scrum Master serves the Organisation in several ways including:</p> <ul> <li>Leading and coaching the organisation in its Scrum adoption Planning the Scrum implementations within the Organisation</li> <li>helping employees and stakeholders understand and enact Scrum and empirical product development </li> <li>Causing change that increases the productivity of the Team and Working with other Scrum Masters to increase the effectiveness of the application of Scrum in the organisation. </li> </ul> <p>Skills/Technologies:</p> <ul> <li>Jira</li> <li>Confluence</li> <li>Agile methodologies &amp; </div><div class="visareqtext"></div><div class="clear"></div><div id="md_skills" class="md_skills"><p><strong>Open Source/Governance Analyst</strong> <br>Our client, a global blue chip organisation are currently looking for an Open Source/Governance Analyst. This position will act as the go-to person and subject matter expert for open source technologies for our client. You will be reporting in to the head of enterprise architecture and work alongside other talented people focusing on technology governance.The successful candidate will combine technical knowledge with business acumen to work with internal and external stakeholders to provide visibility and accountability to the use of open-source. This position requires a strong understanding of open source technologies, leadership, and the ability to communicate effectively with a broad range of stakeholders.</p> <p><strong>Duties included:-</strong> <br>o Lead open source governance as a member of the enterprise architecture team.<br>o Lead the open source policy and open source licensing risk.<br>o Monitoring the client's compliance with open source policy.<br>o Ensure there is a streamlined, well-governed and self-service process and tooling to scan open source vulnerabilities.<br>o Partner with internal legal counsel to manage open source license risk.<br>o Contribute technical expertise for the use of open source technologies.<br>o Understand our current processes and identify where optimization and modernization are required.<br>o Work with Global Sourcing as needed to interpret open-source clauses in supplier contracts and advise if there is any concern with the language presented given the intended use-case.<br>o Work with technology due diligence teams for potential acquisitions to ensure that an independent third-party scan is performed of Target Company's code prior to acquisition.</p> <p><strong>Education:-</strong><br>o Bachelor's Degree or four or more years of work experience.<br>o Four or more years of experience in relevant work experience.</p> <p><strong>Essential Knowledge and Skills:-</strong><br>o Experience contributing to open source and regularly follows developments in the open-source space (eg industry news and developments, new open-source licenses, court cases related violations of open source licenses)<br>o Familiarity with open source governance policies and the reasons for them.<br>o Familiarity with software development processes and tools (eg GitHub, TFS, Jenkins, JIRA, etc.) and understanding of engineering best practices, agile and waterfall methodologies<br>o Strong interpersonal skills supported by expressive oral and written communication styles.<br>o Experience working with various business stakeholders.<br>o Excellent understanding of technology and software development processes.<br>o A desire for continuous learning.<br>o Excellent communication (verbal and writing), influencing and negotiation skills.<br>o Detail-oriented with good organisation skills, communication skills, general business and project management skills.</p> <p><strong>Desirable Knowledge and Skills:- </strong><br>o Previous experience as a developer with any major technology areas like .Net/Java, RESTful and SOAP web services, JavaScript, database technologies.<br>o Knowledge of Black Duck.<br>o Deep understanding of open source license requirements and the impact of those requirements when integrated with closed- source code.</p> <p>Please e-mail your details into Hayley for an immediate interview.</p></div><!-- skills --><div class="clear"></div><div id="jd_mediaUrl" class="jd_mediaUrl"></div><div class="clear"></div><hr><!-- these are </div><div class="visareqtext"><span id="md_visareq" class="md_visareq" style="color:#00aa00">Applicants who require a work visa welcomed</span></div><div class="clear"></div><div id="md_skills" class="md_skills"><p><strong>Business Analyst - Financial Services</strong></p><p><strong>Milton Keynes</strong></p><p><strong>2 Months initially</strong></p><p>As a Business Analyst, you will be involved in all aspects of business and systems analysis work for business projects, programmes and other operational change initiatives. </p><p>You will forge close working relationships with the business and act as the 'bridge' between the business and IT. Your role will involve working closely with the business to gather, analyse and translate specific needs to produce clear, unambiguous business requirements and functional specification documents for IT changes. You will identify organisational impacts, define and document business process changes and will work closely with the Business Transition and Business Performance Improvement teams to manage these impacts.</p><p><strong>Role Overview: </strong></p><ul><li>Working on a New Finance Platform project - a very large project working at a fast pace</li><li>Initially to pull data together and create user stories to enable the project to commence in the new year</li></ul><p><strong>Essential Skills:</strong></p><ul><li>Agile BA project delivery - writing user stories, agile ceremonies</li><li>Strong stakeholder management - will be working with a wide range of stakeholders at different levels of seniority</li></ul><p><strong>Desirable Skills:</strong></p><ul><li>Experience working with Jira</li><li>Financial services experience</li><li>Experience working with external suppliers</li></ul><p><strong>Suitable candidates should submit their CV in the first instance.</strong></p></div><!-- skills --><div class="clear"></div><div id="jd_mediaUrl" class="jd_mediaUrl"></div><div class="clear"></div><hr><!-- these are the individual job detail headers (labels and actual job detail) --><div class="md_items">
